                               '<tr> <td> </td></tr></tbody></table>\n'
                               '<h2>History</h2>\n'
                               '<p>Main article: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human_history">Human '
                               'history</a></p>\n'
                               '<h3>Prehistory</h3>\n'
                               '<p>Main article: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prehistory">Prehistory</a></p>\n'
                               '<figure><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Early_migrations_mercator.svg"><img '
                               'data-file-height="569" data-file-width="1173" '
                               'src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Early_migrations_mercator.svg/660px-Early_migrations_mercator.svg.png" '
                               'srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Early_migrations_mercator.svg/495px-Early_migrations_mercator.svg.png '
                               '1.5x, '
                               '//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8b/Early_migrations_mercator.svg/660px-Early_migrations_mercator.svg.png '
                               '2x"></img></a><figcaption>Overview of the '
                               'peopling of the world by <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Early_human_migrations">early '
                               'human migration</a> during the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Paleolithic">Upper '
                               'Paleolithic</a>, following the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Dispersal">Southern '
                               'Dispersal</a> paradigm</figcaption></figure>\n'
                               '<p>Until about 12,000 years ago, all humans '
                               'lived as <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunter-gatherer">hunter-gatherers</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> '
                               'The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neolithic_Revolution">Neolithic '
                               'Revolution</a> (the invention of <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Agriculture">agriculture</a>) '
                               'first took place in <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southwest_Asia">Southwest '
                               'Asia</a> and spread through large parts of the '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_World">Old '
                               'World</a> over the following millennia.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> '
                               'It also occurred independently in <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mesoamerica">Mesoamerica</a> '
                               '(about 6,000 years ago),<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> '
                               'China,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea">Papua '
                               'New Guinea</a>,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sahel">Sahel</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudanian_savanna">West '
                               'Savanna</a> regions of Africa.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<p>Access to food surplus led to the formation '
                               'of permanent <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human_settlement">human '
                               'settlements</a>, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domestication">domestication</a> '
                               'of animals and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chalcolithic">use '
                               'of metal tools</a> for the first time in '
                               'history. Agriculture and sedentary lifestyle '
                               'led to the emergence of early <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Civilizations">civilizations</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<h3>Ancient</h3>\n'
                               '<p>Main article: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_history">Ancient '
                               'history</a></p>\n'
                               '<figure><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg"><img '
                               'data-file-height="2906" data-file-width="4372" '
                               'src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg/440px-All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg" '
                               'srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg/330px-All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg '
                               '1.5x, '
                               '//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg/440px-All_Gizah_Pyramids.jpg '
                               '2x"></img></a><figcaption><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Giza_pyramid_complex">Great '
                               'Pyramids of Giza</a>, '
                               'Egypt</figcaption></figure>\n'
                               '<p>An <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urban_revolution">urban '
                               'revolution</a> took place in the 4th '
                               'millennium BCE with the development of <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/City-state">city-states</a>, '
                               'particularly <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sumer">Sumerian</a> '
                               'cities located in <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mesopotamia">Mesopotamia</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-64">[64]</a></sup> '
                               'It was in these cities that the earliest known '
                               'form of writing, <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cuneiform_script">cuneiform '
                               'script</a>, appeared around 3000 BCE.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup> '
                               'Other major civilizations to develop around '
                               'this time were <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Egypt">Ancient '
                               'Egypt</a> and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indus_Valley_Civilisation">Indus '
                               'Valley Civilisation</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup> '
                               'They eventually traded with each other and '
                               'invented technology such as wheels, plows and '
                               'sails.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-Bodnár-2018-68">[68]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-69">[69]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-70">[70]</a></sup> '
                               'Emerging by 3000 BCE, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caral%E2%80%93Supe_civilization">Caral&ndash;Supe '
                               'civilization</a> is the oldest complex '
                               'civilization in the Americas.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> '
                               'Astronomy and mathematics were also developed '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Pyramid_of_Giza">Great '
                               'Pyramid of Giza</a> was built.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-72">[72]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-73">[73]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-74">[74]</a></sup> '
                               'There is evidence of a <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/4.2-kiloyear_event">severe '
                               'drought</a> lasting about a hundred years that '
                               'may have caused the decline of these '
                               'civilizations,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-75">[75]</a></sup> '
                               'with new ones appearing in the aftermath. <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Babylonia">Babylonians</a> '
                               'came to dominate Mesopotamia while '
                               'others,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-76">[76]</a></sup> '
                               'such as the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poverty_Point_culture">Poverty '
                               'Point culture</a>, <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Minoan_civilization">Minoans</a> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shang_dynasty">Shang '
                               'dynasty</a>, rose to prominence in new '
                               'areas.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-77">[77]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-78">[78]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-79">[79]</a></sup> '
                               'The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Bronze_Age_collapse">Late '
                               'Bronze Age collapse</a> around 1200 BCE '
                               'resulted in the disappearance of a number of '
                               'civilizations and the beginning of the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_Dark_Ages">Greek '
                               'Dark Ages</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-80">[80]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-81">[81]</a></sup> '
                               'During this period iron started replacing '
                               'bronze, leading to the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iron_Age">Iron '
                               'Age</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-82">[82]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<p>In the 5th century BCE, history started '
                               'being <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Historiography">recorded '
                               'as a discipline</a>, which provided a much '
                               'clearer picture of life at the time.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-83">[83]</a></sup> '
                               'Between the 8th and 6th century BCE, Europe '
                               'entered the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_antiquity">classical '
                               'antiquity</a> age, a period when <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greece">ancient '
                               'Greece</a> and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Rome">ancient '
                               'Rome</a> flourished.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-84">[84]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-85">[85]</a></sup> '
                               'Around this time other civilizations also came '
                               'to prominence. The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_civilization">Maya '
                               'civilization</a> started to build cities and '
                               'create <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_calendar">complex '
                               'calendars</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-86">[86]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-87">[87]</a></sup> '
                               'In Africa, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Aksum">Kingdom '
                               'of Aksum</a> overtook the declining <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Kush">Kingdom '
                               'of Kush</a> and facilitated trade between '
                               'India and the Mediterranean.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-88">[88]</a></sup> '
                               'In West Asia, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Achaemenid_Empire">Achaemenid '
                               "Empire</a>'s system of centralized governance "
                               'became the precursor to many later '
                               'empires,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-89">[89]</a></sup> '
                               'while the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gupta_Empire">Gupta '
                               'Empire</a> in India and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Han_dynasty">Han '
                               'dynasty</a> in China have been described as <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Golden_ages">golden '
                               'ages</a> in their respective regions.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-90">[90]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-91">[91]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<h3>Medieval</h3>\n'
                               '<p>Main article: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Post-classical_history">Post-classical '
                               'history</a></p>\n'
                               '<figure><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg"><img '
                               'data-file-height="1262" data-file-width="1278" '
                               'src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg/340px-Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg" '
                               'srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg/255px-Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg '
                               '1.5x, '
                               '//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg/340px-Cleric-Knight-Workman.jpg '
                               '2x"></img></a><figcaption>Medieval French <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Illuminated_manuscript">manuscript '
                               'illustration</a> of the three <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Social_class">classes</a> '
                               'of medieval society from the 13th-century '
                               '<i>Li Livres dou '
                               'Sant&eacute;</i></figcaption></figure>\n'
                               '<p>Following the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fall_of_the_Western_Roman_Empire">fall '
                               'of the Western Roman Empire</a> in 476, Europe '
                               'entered the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Ages">Middle '
                               'Ages</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup> '
                               'During this period, <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christianity">Christianity</a> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catholic_Church">Church</a> '
                               'would provide centralized authority and '
                               'education.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> '
                               'In the Middle East, <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islam">Islam</a> '
                               'became the prominent religion and expanded '
                               'into North Africa. It led to an <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islamic_Golden_Age">Islamic '
                               'Golden Age</a>, inspiring achievements in <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Architecture">architecture</a>, '
                               'the revival of old advances in science and '
                               'technology, and the formation of a distinct '
                               'way of life.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-Renima-2016-94">[94]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> '
                               'The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christendom">Christian</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Islamic_world">Islamic '
                               'worlds</a> would eventually clash, with the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_England">Kingdom '
                               'of England</a>, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_France">Kingdom '
                               'of France</a> and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holy_Roman_Empire">Holy '
                               'Roman Empire</a> declaring a series of <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crusades">holy '
                               'wars</a> to regain control of the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holy_Land">Holy '
                               'Land</a> from <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muslim">Muslims</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<p>In the Americas, between 200 and 900 CE <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mesoamerica">Mesoamerica</a> '
                               'was in its <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mesoamerican_chronology#Classic_Period">Classic '
                               'Period</a>,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-97">[97]</a></sup> '
                               'while further north, complex <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mississippian_culture">Mississippian '
                               'societies</a> would arise starting around 800 '
                               'CE.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup> '
                               'The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongol_Empire">Mongol '
                               'Empire</a> would conquer much of <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eurasia">Eurasia</a> '
                               'in the 13th and 14th centuries.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup> '
                               'Over this same time period, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mali_Empire">Mali '
                               'Empire</a> in Africa grew to be the largest '
                               'empire on the continent, stretching from <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Senegambia">Senegambia</a> '
                               'to <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ivory_Coast">Ivory '
                               'Coast</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup> '
                               'Oceania would see the rise of the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tu%CA%BBi_Tonga_Empire">Tuʻi '
                               'Tonga Empire</a> which expanded across many '
                               'islands in the South Pacific.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup> '
                               'By the late 15th century, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aztecs">Aztecs</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Inca">Inca</a> '
                               'had become the dominant power in Mesoamerica '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andean_civilizations">Andes</a>, '
                               'respectively.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<h3>Modern</h3>\n'
                               '<p>Main articles: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Early_modern_period">Early '
                               'modern period</a> and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_modern_period">Late '
                               'modern period</a></p>\n'
                               '<figure><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg"><img '
                               'data-file-height="760" data-file-width="1024" '
                               'src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg/440px-Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg" '
                               'srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg/330px-Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg '
                               '1.5x, '
                               '//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg/440px-Maquina_vapor_Watt_ETSIIM.jpg '
                               '2x"></img></a><figcaption><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Watt">James '
                               "Watt</a>'s steam engine</figcaption></figure>\n"
                               '<p>The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Early_modern_period">early '
                               'modern period</a> in Europe and the Near East '
                               '(c. 1450&ndash;1800) began with the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fall_of_Constantinople">final '
                               'defeat of the Byzantine Empire</a>, and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Empire">rise '
                               'of the Ottoman Empire</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup> '
                               'Meanwhile, Japan entered the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edo_period">Edo '
                               'period</a>,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup> '
                               'the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Qing_dynasty">Qing '
                               'dynasty</a> rose in China<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mughal_Empire">Mughal '
                               'Empire</a> ruled much of India.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup> '
                               'Europe underwent the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Renaissance">Renaissance</a>, '
                               'starting in the 15th century,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Age_of_Discovery">Age '
                               'of Discovery</a> began with the exploring and '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colonialism">colonizing</a> '
                               'of new regions.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup> '
                               'This included the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_colonization_of_the_Americas">colonization '
                               'of the Americas</a><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Columbian_Exchange">Columbian '
                               'Exchange</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup> '
                               'This expansion led to the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlantic_slave_trade">Atlantic '
                               'slave trade</a><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Genocide_of_Native_Americans">genocide '
                               'of Native American peoples</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> '
                               'This period also marked the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scientific_Revolution">Scientific '
                               'Revolution</a>, with great advances in <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mathematics">mathematics</a>, '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mechanics">mechanics</a>, '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Astronomy">astronomy</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Physiology">physiology</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<p>The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_modern_period">late '
                               'modern period</a> (1800&ndash;present) saw the '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Technological_Revolution">Technological</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Industrial_Revolution">Industrial '
                               'Revolution</a> bring such discoveries as <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imaging_technology">imaging '
                               'technology</a>, major innovations in transport '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Energy_development">energy '
                               'development</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> '
                               'Influenced by <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Age_of_Enlightenment">Enlightenment</a> '
                               'ideals, the Americas and Europe experienced a '
                               'period of political revolutions known as the '
                               '<a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Age_of_Revolution">Age '
                               'of Revolution</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup> '
                               'The <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Napoleonic_Wars">Napoleonic '
                               'Wars</a> raged through Europe in the early '
                               '1800s,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup> '
                               'Spain lost most of its colonies in the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_World">New '
                               'World</a>,<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup> '
                               'while Europeans continued <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scramble_for_Africa">expansion '
                               'into Africa</a> &ndash; where European control '
                               'went from 10% to almost 90% in less than 50 '
                               'years<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup> '
                               '&ndash; and Oceania.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-119">[119]</a></sup> '
                               'In the 19th century, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Empire">British '
                               'Empire</a> expanded to become the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_largest_empires">world\'s '
                               'largest empire</a>.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<figure><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg"><img '
                               'data-file-height="3816" data-file-width="5088" '
                               'src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg/440px-Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg" '
                               'srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg/330px-Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg '
                               '1.5x, '
                               '//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg/440px-Schenker_VIA14_Laptop_asv2021-01.jpg '
                               '2x"></img></a><figcaption>A laptop connected '
                               'to the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet">Internet</a>.</figcaption></figure>\n'
                               '<p>A tenuous <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balance_of_power_(international_relations)">balance '
                               'of power</a> among European nations collapsed '
                               'in 1914 with the outbreak of the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_I">First '
                               'World War</a>, one of the deadliest conflicts '
                               'in history.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup> '
                               'In the 1930s, <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Depression">a '
                               'worldwide economic crisis</a> led to the rise '
                               'of <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Authoritarian">authoritarian</a> '
                               'regimes and a <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II">Second '
                               'World War</a>, involving <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II_by_country">almost '
                               "all of the world's countries</a>.<sup><a "
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> '
                               "The war's destruction led to the collapse of "
                               'most global empires, leading to widespread '
                               'decolonization.</p>\n'
                               '<p>Following the conclusion of the Second '
                               'World War in 1945, the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States">United '
                               'States</a><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-123">[123]</a></sup> '
                               'and the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USSR">USSR</a> '
                               'emerged as the remaining <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Global_superpower">global '
                               'superpowers</a>. This led to a <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cold_War">Cold '
                               'War</a> that saw a struggle for global '
                               'influence, including a <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuclear_arms_race">nuclear '
                               'arms race</a> and a <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Space_Race">space '
                               'race</a>, ending in the collapse of the Soviet '
                               'Union.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-124">[124]</a></sup><sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-125">[125]</a></sup> '
                               'The current <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Information_Age">Information '
                               'Age</a>, spurred by the development of the <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet">Internet</a> '
                               'and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artificial_intelligence">artificial '
                               'intelligence</a> systems, sees the world '
                               'becoming increasingly <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Globalization">globalized</a> '
                               'and interconnected.<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup></p>\n'
                               '<h2>Habitat and population</h2>\n'
                               '<p>Further information: <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human_geography">Human '
                               'geography</a> and <a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Demography">Demography</a></p>\n'
                               '<table>Population statistics<sup><a '
                               'href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human#cite_note-129">[n '
                               '1]</a></sup><tbody><tr><td '
